Subject: [dm-l] Closing conference of the project ANR ALIENTO - presentation

Dear colleagues,

We are please to announce the programme of the 7th edition of the 
Aliento Conference. We invite you to the presentation of the database, 
which will open to all January, 2018.

Best regards,

Marie-Sol Ortola (UdL), Marie-Christine Bornes Varol (Inalco), Benjamin 
Husson (atilf)
